-- USERS TABLE
CREATE TABLE users (
    user_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    user_dob DATE NOT NULL,
    user_gender VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    user_email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    user_phone_number VARCHAR(15) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    user_address TEXT
);


-- GUARDIANS TABLE
CREATE TABLE guardians (
    guardian_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    guardian_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    guardian_phone_number VARCHAR(15) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    guardian_email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    guardian_address TEXT,
    user_id INT
);


ALTER TABLE guardians
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_guardians_users
FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id);


-- DOCTORS TABLE
CREATE TABLE doctors (
    doctor_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    doctor_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    doctor_specialty VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    doctor_hospital VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    doctor_contact_info VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL
);


-- USERDOCTOR TABLE
CREATE TABLE userdoctor (
    user_id INT not null,
    doctor_id INT not null,
    last_visit_date DATE,
    notes TEXT
);


ALTER TABLE userdoctor
add CONSTRAINT pk_userdoctor
PRIMARY KEY (user_id, doctor_id);


ALTER TABLE userdoctor
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_userdoctor_users
FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id);


ALTER TABLE userdoctor
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_userdoctor_doctors
FOREIGN KEY (doctor_id) REFERENCES doctors(doctor_id);


-- SMARTWATCHES TABLE
CREATE TABLE smartwatches (
    data_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INT
);


ALTER TABLE smartwatches
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_smartwatches_users
FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id);
GO


CREATE PROCEDURE InsertHealthData
    @data_id INT,
    @user_id INT,
    @heart_rate INT,
    @blood_oxygen_level INT,
    @sleep_duration_hours FLOAT,
    @step_count INT,
    @activity_level VARCHAR(20),
    @stress_level VARCHAR(20)
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;


    -- Insert into healthdata table
    INSERT INTO healthdata (
        data_id, user_id, heart_rate, blood_oxygen_level,
        sleep_duration_hours, step_count, activity_level, stress_level
    )
    VALUES (
        @data_id, @user_id, @heart_rate, @blood_oxygen_level,
        @sleep_duration_hours, @step_count, @activity_level, @stress_level
    );


    -- Generate alert if health thresholds are exceeded
    IF (@heart_rate > 100 OR @blood_oxygen_level < 92 or @sleep_duration_hours<6 or @stress_level >7)
    BEGIN
        INSERT INTO alerts (
            alert_id,
            user_id,
            alert_severity,
            data_id
        )
        VALUES (
            ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 100000 + 9000,
            @user_id,
            CASE 
                WHEN @heart_rate > 100 THEN 'High Heart Rate'
                WHEN @heart_rate < 60 THEN 'Low Heart Rate'
                WHEN @blood_oxygen_level < 92 THEN 'Low Blood Oxygen Level'
                WHEN @sleep_duration_hours<6 THEN 'Insufficient Sleep'
                WHEN @stress_level >7 THEN 'High Stress Level'
                ELSE null 
            END,
            @data_id
        );
    END
END
GO 




-- HEALTHDATA TABLE
CREATE TABLE healthdata (
    data_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INT,
    heart_rate INT,
    blood_oxygen_level INT,
    sleep_duration_hours FLOAT,
    step_count INT,
    activity_level VARCHAR(20),
    stress_level VARCHAR(20)
);


ALTER TABLE healthdata
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_healthdata_users
FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id);










-- ALERTS TABLE
CREATE TABLE alerts (
    alert_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INT,
    data_id INT not null,
    alert_severity VARCHAR(20)
);


ALTER TABLE alerts
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_alerts_users
FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id);


ALTER TABLE alerts
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_alerts_data
FOREIGN KEY (data_id) REFERENCES healthdata(data_id);




drop PROCEDURE if exists ProcessHealthData
GO


CREATE OR ALTER PROCEDURE ProcessHealthData
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;


    -- Generate alerts for healthdata that meet conditions
    INSERT INTO alerts (
        alert_id,
        user_id,
        alert_severity,
        data_id
    )
    SELECT 
        (SELECT ISNULL(MAX(alert_id), 0) FROM alerts) + ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY (SELECT NULL)) alert_id,
        user_id,
        CASE
            WHEN heart_rate > 100 THEN 'High Heart Rate'
            WHEN heart_rate < 60 THEN 'Low Heart Rate'
            WHEN blood_oxygen_level < 92 THEN 'Low Blood Oxy'
            WHEN sleep_duration_hours < 6 THEN 'Insufficient Sleep'
            WHEN stress_level > 7 THEN 'High Stress Level'
        END AS alert_severity,
        data_id
    FROM healthdata
    WHERE 
        heart_rate > 100 
        OR heart_rate < 60
        OR blood_oxygen_level < 92
        OR sleep_duration_hours < 6
        OR stress_level > 7;
END;
GO


EXECUTE ProcessHealthData
